    & & & \multicolumn{2}{p{0.3\linewidth}}{
        \cellcolor[rgb]{0.9,0.9,0.9}{
            \makecell[{{p{\linewidth}}}]{
                \texttt{\tiny{[GM$|$GM]}}
                {'goal_states_achieved': ['at(potion1,kitchen1)'], 'game_successfully_finished': True}
            }
        }
    }
    & & \\ \\

\end{supertabular}
}
